name:lâ€aâ€oâ€zâ€hâ€aâ€n
info:Executive Floor Deluxe King Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Business travelers
info:33 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 5, 2024
msg:I have already reviewed the room part, and this review mainly focuses on the breakfast part.
One of the reasons why I have stayed at Wanda Realm Zengcheng Hotel for so long is that its breakfast is very rich and worthy of the name of Gourmet Place.
The breakfast room is on the first floor of the hotel, behind the front desk. The restaurant is very large and can accommodate more than 150 people at the same time. Anyway, after eating there for so many days, I have never seen the breakfast room full.
There is a noodle stall on the left side of the door. I tried its Zhengguo wontons and they tasted pretty good. Then there is the dinner area, which generally has at least one fried noodles and fried rice, and five or six dishes. What I am more satisfied with is that there are more vegetables, which are actually harder to eat outside. Then there is the porridge section, there are generally five kinds, white porridge, millet porridge, beef porridge and soy milk are must-haves, and then there are various pickles on the side. If I choose porridge, I will add mustard; if it is soy milk, it will add sugar and honey. But I havenâ€™t tried soy milk with honey. After the porridge, there is a mobile steamed bun cart. There are relatively few steamed buns and pastries here. One steamer is for barbecued pork buns, and the other is often for corn and potatoes. Bacon is usually placed in a mobile manner. Sometimes it is placed in front of the dinner area. Sometimes it is placed next to the steamed stuffed bun cart. At the end of the passage is the egg stall, which is more interesting. There are all kinds of eggs, hard-boiled eggs, tea eggs, poached eggs, and there are two types: sun-cooked eggs and relatively cooked poached eggs. There are also egg cakes, and there are requirements for egg cakes. Add various toppings. Behind the egg stall is usually a yogurt shop.
In addition to the dining counter next to the main aisle, there are two dining counters in the middle of the seating area. These two dining counters are the first places I go to every day. One dining counter mainly sells Western pastries. Swiss rolls, waffles and cream meal packs, as long as they are available, I will basically get them. The waffles also come with four kinds of sauces. I also take turns adding the toppings every day. The other dining station has more things, mainly fruits, salads and For drinks and fruits, cantaloupe and dragon fruit are good, watermelon is just average, and there are other fruits in summer that I can't name, all of which are freshly cut. I usually eat salads, add some vegetables or potatoes, and drinks include various milks and juices. Juices are usually placed in ice boxes, but there are some hot water bottles next to the coffee machine, which includes lemon tea and boiled water. , I will add a little bit to the ice juice to adjust the temperature.
Anyway, whenever I stay in Zengcheng Wanda, I can eat all-you-can-eat breakfast at Food Club every day. I have never been hungry or tired of eating it for so many days. This is really not easy.
